work!\r\n\r\nThe Kanban methodology:\r\nTasks are represented by Kanbans which are added to the Kanban board and then worked on. Do NOT place too much Tasks at once (!) in the TO_DO state! Dont promise to do what you can't do! Less is more. Kanbans are moved across the board to the IN_PROGRES queue and worked on until the are completed and then moved to the final completed (\"DONE\") queue.\r\n\r\n\r\nBoards:\r\nA Kanban \"board\" literally can represent everything you want it to be: a simple shopping list, a work project, an event, you know... everything.\r\n\r\n\r\nTasks and their States:\r\nYou assign your Tasks to a Board. BTW: the DONE state is your favorite state  :-)\r\n\r\nOn every Board there is another State: the OVERDUE state.  That's the worst state of all. If possible, it is recommended to avoiding the \"overdue\" state   ;)\r\n\r\nYou can NOT manually (via drag&drop) move a Task to the OVERDUE column. That will not work.  A Task will be automatically placed in the OVERDUE column when it's overdue date (required field when creating a new task) has been reached.\r\n\r\nHowever, when you've finished your already-should-have-been-done Task you can quite simply move it via drag and drop to the DONE column. processing of personal data and on the free movement of such data, and repealing Directive 95/46/EC (General Data Protection Regulation - GDPR).\r\n\r\nThe application can be used as a stand-alone solution or as part of the enterprise cyber protection system  (system BS-1421R).\r\n\r\n\r\nCUSTOMIZABLE AND EASY\r\n\r\nWorking with FPS does not require special knowledge. The interface is intuitive. Working with the application is very similar to that of File Explorer. Users can choose between a large number of encryption algorithms. Settings can be saved, which allows customization of the system.\r\n\r\n\r\nAVAILABLE VERSIONS\r\n\r\n - Free Edition - Limited Edition version. corporations.\r\n\r\n\r\nENCRYPTION ALGORITHMS AND HASH FUNCTIONS\r\n\r\nThe application includes the following standard encryption algorithms: \r\n\r\nAdvanced Encryption Standard (block size of 128 Un serveur VPN auquel vous vous connectez, par exemple via le VPN Hotspot Shield, établit une connexion chiffrée, et sécurisée, à un serveur situé dans un autre pays. Grâce à ce chiffrement, les données transmises ne peuvent être ni filtrées ni bloquées. \r\n\r\n* Pourquoi utiliser un VPN ?\r\nUn VPN ne permet pas seulement d'accéder à des services censurés ou bloqués, comme Facebook, Pandora ou YouTube, mais vous bénéficiez également d'une sécurité et d'une confidentialité en ligne optimales. Vous pouvez surfer sur le web anonymement et en toute sécurité.\r\n\r\n* Comparaison VPN / Proxy\r\nUn VPN et un proxy peuvent tous deux empêcher votre identification en redirigeant votre trafic internet et en modifiant votre adresse IP. À l'inverse, un service VPN chiffre tout votre trafic et fonctionne avec tous les services basés sur internet.
